msg:In October of the golden autumn, I took my parents to Beijing Yanqi Hotel again. Yanqi Hotel is located in Yanqi Lake, Huairou, Beijing. It was built for the Asia-Pacific Economic Cooperation conference. It was opened to the outside world after the conference and became a garden-style luxury hotel suitable for leisure. It includes villas and hotels. This time we stayed at hotel standards. between. When traveling, food, accommodation and transportation are the most important experiences. Let me talk about my experience this time. The first thing is to eat. There are three meals a day, breakfast, lunch and dinner. Let‚Äôs talk about breakfast first. There are many kinds, a combination of Chinese and Western, which is the standard of a luxury five-star hotel. I have been eating Western-style breakfast for a few days, so let‚Äôs talk about it. There are many kinds of bread, including French baguettes, farmer‚Äôs bread, brown bread, and various toast breads; eggs include fried eggs, boiled eggs, and braised eggs; cheeses include Swiss cheese. There are hard cheeses such as French cheese, Dutch blue cheese, and cheddar cheese, as well as soft cheeses such as French Brie and King Wen, but the amount of soft cheese is small and will be gone if you go late; meats include bacon, ham, All kinds of meat sausages; the unique thing is that it has a burger DIY area, which puts all the raw materials for burgers together for you to choose freely. Lunch and dinner are all Chinese food, mainly Cantonese cuisine, which is quite satisfactory and has no outstanding features. What is distinctive is its soup, which is very well prepared and heated enough, and it is all clear soup. Its dishes use soup everywhere. It is the stock that enhances the taste of the dish. Secondly, it‚Äôs accommodation. This time we stayed in a garden-view balcony room, which was fully equipped and equipped with a coffee machine. You can make your own coffee. The drinks in the refrigerator are free, and you can also ask the waiter to deliver ice cubes. Third, speaking of travel, Yanqi Hotel is on Yanqi Island. Vehicles must be registered in advance before entering, and the management is strict, which is very good. More than 80% of the island's green area is green, and Yanqi Lake is vast. There is also a pocket garden surrounding Yanqi Tower in the hotel courtyard, which makes wandering in the center of it refreshing. The hotel also provides bicycles for riding in the park, and you can also go up to the Yanqi Tower to enjoy the distance. The hotel also provides boat tours to Yanqi Lake. To sum up, I think Yanqi Hotel is the best choice for vacation and leisure hotels around Beijing. Worth a visit for everyone.
